			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In the second </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fiscal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarter, w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">hile we saw</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> double digit</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> growth in our Americas segment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which has already moved through</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">price-increase related</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> disruptions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. O</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ur EMEA and Asia-Pacific segments reported sales that were softer than we would like to see. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The disruptions we have been experiencing in EMEA are due primarily to recent pric</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">e-increase </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">actions coupled with our loss of sales in Russia and Belarus. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Asia-Pacific</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> segment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">we experienced some</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="font-family:Segoe UI;font-size:9pt;display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;color:#000000;">weaker economic conditions and pricing disruptions in our distributor markets.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">However, we are expecting a strong comeback in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">both </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">EMEA</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and Asia-Pacific</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the second half of the fiscal year.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Although gross margin in the second quarter improved compared to the same period last year, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">there continues to be pressure on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">gross margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. Progress is </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">seldom</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">linear,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and many factors</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> are currently</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> impact</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ing</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> gross margin. The good news is that</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">e are beginning to see input costs stabilize and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> inventory levels come down</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> We</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> are hopeful that </font>
		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"></font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"></font>

		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			&nbsp;

				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;;"> &#xB7;</font>

		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales by segment as a percent of total net sale</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s for </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter were as follows: for the Americas, 4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent; for EMEA, 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> for Asia-Pacific, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">16</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">percent.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in the Americas increased 15 percent in the second quarter due primarily to higher sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;o</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">f</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">maintenance products in the United States, which increased 22 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. Increased maintenance product sales were d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">riven</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">by</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the impact of price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> increased production capacity</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and improved </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">availability of certain products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. These increases were partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">lower demand which resulted in decreased sales volume.</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In Canada, sales increased 10 percent due to the favorable impact of price increases partially offset by unfavorable changes in foreign currency exchange rates and weaker economic conditions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">that resulted in lower levels of demand and decreased sales volume.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In Latin America, sales increased by 3 percent primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to higher sales in our direct market in Mexico as a result of increased distribution, successful promotional programs and price increases, as well as the favorable impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates.&nbsp;&nbsp;These favorable impacts were significantly offset by decreased sales volumes to marketing distributors in Latin America due to weaker economic conditions in certain regions that resulted in lower levels of demand.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA decreased 13 percent in the second quarter primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to changes </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in foreign currency exchange rates, which had an unfavorable impact on sales for the EMEA segment in the second quarter compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. On a constant currency basis, EMEA sales for the second quarter would have decreased by 4 percent compared to the prior fiscal year quarter. In addition, decreases in sales volume unfavorably impacted sales of maintenance products in the EMEA, which was significantly offset by the favorable impact of price increases we implemented over the last twelve months. Direct market sales were unfavorably impacted by a lower level of customer orders, partially due to weaker market and economic conditions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which have led to reduced foot traffic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in most regions and a lower level of promotional programs, partially offset by the favorable impact of price increases. Lower sales of maintenance products in the EMEA distributor markets were primarily attributable to the suspension in sales of our products to our marketing distributor customers in Russia and Belarus starting in March of 2022.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">lower</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales of maintenance products in the Asia-Pacific distributor markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which decreased 11 percent in the second quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. Lower</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales of maintenance products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the Asia-Pacific distributor markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> were </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily due to lower sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE; &nbsp;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Multi-Use Product driven by weaker market and economic conditions and distributors that had purchased product in advance of price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> implemented in December 2022</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, both of which lowered sales volumes in the second quarter of fiscal year 2023, particularly in Taiwan, Korea, Thailand and Malaysia</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. In China, sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">remained </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">relatively constant period </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> period.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In Australia</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased by 6 percent primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to the favorable impact of price increases and successful promotional programs.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had an unfavorable impact on sales for the Asia-Pacific segment. On a constant currency basis, Asia-Pacific sales would have </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Dividend and Share Repurchase Update</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">March</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">21</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">a &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">regular </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">quarterly dividend of $0.83 per share payable on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">April 28</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 2023 to stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">April</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> &nbsp;1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">, 2023.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">On October 12, 2021, the Company&#x2019;s </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">b</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">oard of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">irectors approved a share buy-back plan that became effective on November 1, 2021. Under the plan</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> the Company is authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares through August 31, 2023. The timing and amount of repurchases will be based on terms and conditions acceptable to the Company and in c</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">ompliance with applicable laws and regulations. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">During the period from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">November 1, 2021 through </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">February</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">28</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, the Company repurchased&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">170,232</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> shares at a total cost of&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">34.8 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">million under this $75.0 million plan.</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">During the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter, the Company repurchased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">9,250</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> shares at a total cost of&#x202F;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x202F;million under this $75.0 million plan.</font>
		</p>
